msg:It is very close to the ancient city. I always walk there. The service staff are very good. If there is any problem, they will solve it for you as soon as possible. The price of more than 200 yuan per night is worth it for off-peak travel. OK, now let me talk about the strange experience in the hotel. At the beginning, I checked into Room 567 in the afternoon. I put my luggage in the room and went out to the ancient city. When I came back at night, I found that the noise was very loud without turning on the air conditioner. It was the noise from the hotel's air conditioning duct. I reported it to the front desk staff and immediately arranged someone to come and see. They said that there was no noise after the facility was turned off at 11 o'clock. I thought about making do with it for one night and asking the hotel to change the room the next day. As a result, I waited until 11 o'clock and found that the noise was gone, and the air conditioner was gone. I asked the front desk to tell me that their hotel would turn off the air conditioner at 11 o'clock. This is the first time I have encountered such a strange rule in so many years. I originally stayed for three consecutive nights, and I couldn't stand it. I found the website customer service and asked to cancel the next two nights. After communicating with the hotel, the website customer service said that they could send me a fan... Later, the hotel front desk staff also called up and said that if it was cold, they could send me a heater, and if it was hot, they could send me a fan. I asked her, if the air conditioning in this room of your hotel is running, it will be so noisy that I can't sleep without the air conditioning in my room. And then there is no air conditioning at 11 o'clock in the evening, how can I rest? The front desk immediately came up to help me move to the same room on the 7th floor. Here comes the funny thing, the hotel agreed to turn off the air conditioning after 11 o'clock in the evening, but it was not turned off during the few days I lived on the 7th floor. I kept the air conditioning on at night. Does the hotel selectively turn it off? Anyway, I have no complaints about the front desk and the waiters. They really do their job well. It's just that I think there is a big problem with the room at the beginning. Also, there is a flyer for car rental advertisements posted on the ceiling of your room 567? How can it be posted in such a place? I don't understand.
